Privacy Policy (English)

Translation of Privacy Policy for reference

This Privacy Policy is an English Translation of the Korean Privacy Policy, which is used for reference only, and since this effect is in the Korean originia, the English translation has no legal effect.

Greystein Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as the "Company) is the personal information protection regulations in the relevant laws and regulations that information and communication service providers must comply with, such as the Information and Communication Network Promotion and Information Protection Act, Personal Information Protection Act, Communication Secret Protection Act, and Telecommunication Business Act. We are committed to protecting the rights and interests of users by establishing a privacy policy in accordance with relevant laws and regulations.

The privacy policy of Inclass service contains the following contents.

  • 1. Purpose of collection and use of personal information
  • 2. Items of personal information to be collected and collection method
  • 3. Retention and use period of personal information
  • 4. Personal information destruction procedure and method
  • 5. Provision and sharing of personal information
  • 6. Consignment of handling personal information
  • 7. Matters concerning the installation, operation and rejection of automatic personal information collection devices
  • 8. Technical/administrative protection measures for personal information
  • 9. Rights of users and legal representatives and how to exercise them
  • 10. Personal information manager and consultation/report
  • 11. Matters concerning changes to the personal information processing policy
  • 12. Civil service for personal information

1. Purpose of collection and use of personal information

  • 1. Personal information is used for membership registration, provision of services promised to users, purchase and payment, personal authentication according to service provision, delivery of goods and services
  • Member Managment
    • Personal information is used for member management such as membership identification, personal identification, prevention of illegal use and unauthorized use of bad members, confirmation of intention to join, limit on the number subscriptions, confirmation of consent of a legal representative when collecting personal information of children under the age of 14, confirmation of legal representative's identity, record retention for dispute resolution and handling inquiries for complaints.
  • New service development and marketing, utilization of advertisement
    • Development of new services (products) and provision of specialized services, provision of services and advertiesments according to statistical characteristics, identification of access frequency, provision of event information and participation opportunities, provision of advertisement information, provision of information about admission facilities and information of new products, telemarketing, member statistics on service use, etc (Personal information is not provided to the individual or organization that requested the advertisement.)
  • ETC
    • Limiting the number of subscriptions, preserving records for dispute settlement, verifying members' acceptance status, and calculating other statistical data

2. Items of personal information to be collected and collection method

a) Items of personal information to be collected

  • The company collects the minimum personal information by dividing into mandatory and optional items as follows at the time of initial membership registration for membership registration, smooth customer consultation, and provision of various services.
    <Inclass members>
    • Required : Name, ID, Password, Gender, Birth, Phone number, Email, Parent (or legal representative) information if under 14 years of age
    • Optional : Address, Affiliation Information, Sign up Path, Recommended person
  • The following information may be generated and collected during the service use process or business processing process.
    • Content download record, service usage record, access log, cookie, access IP information, payment record, defect usage record
  • In the process of using additional services and customized services or applying for an event, some information may be collected only for the users of the service, and such information will be collected after obtaining consent for separate collection items.
  • The following information may be collected to prevent fraudulent use when using content and some services :
    • MAC Address, HDD Serial, Name of PC
  • In the process of using paid services, the following payment information may be collected :
    • Credit card payment: Payment related records such as card company code, authorization number, etc.
    • Account transfer: Payment related records such as bank code
    • Payment without bankbook: Records related to payment such as virtual account number
    • ARS card payment: Payment related records such as approval number and payment date
    • Mobile phone payment: Payment-related records such as authorization number and carrier code
‚Äª Information subject's right to refuse collection and use and notice of disadvantages

The information subject may refuse to consent to the items and methods of collection of personal information collected by the company, and in the event of refusal, some of the use of services provided to members may be restricted.

b) How to collect personal information

The company collects personal information in the following ways :
  • Homepage, written form, fax, telephone, consultation bulletin board, email, event application, delivery request, etc
  • Online application submission, online information session reservation, parent letter, parent consultation reservation, admission facility name session, questionnaire, etc.
  • Collection through generated information collection tool
  • When collecting personal information over the phone, the content of the call will be recorded and the recording will be notified to the user.

3. Retention and use period of personal information

In principle, the company destroys users' personal information without delay after the purpose of collecting and using personal information is achieved. However, the following information is retained for the specified period for the following reasons:

a) Reasons for information preservation according to company internal policy

  • General member personal information - reason for retention: Prevent confusion and illegal use of the service
    • Retention period: 1 year
  • Service use-related information (service use record, access log, access IP information)
    • Reasons for preservation: Protection of Communications Secrets Act
    • Retention period: 3 months
  • Member personal information using electronic payment
    • Reasons for preservation: Act on Consumer Protection in Electronic Commerce Transactions, etc.
    • Retention period: 5 years
  • Personal information of students and parents collected during entrance examination consulting
    • Reasons for preservation: Consulting history provided upon request, refund, etc.
    • Retention period : 2 years after achievement of purpose (completion of entrance examination consulting)

b) Reasons for information preservation according to related laws

If it is necessary to preserve it in accordance with the provisions of related laws, such as the Commercial Act, the Consumer Protection Act in e-commerce, etc., the company retains the member information for a certain period stipulated by the relevant laws. In this case, the company uses the information to be preserved only for the purpose of its preservation, and the retention period is as follows.
  • Log records on display/advertising
    • Reasons for preservation: Act on Consumer Protection in Electronic Commerce Transactions, etc.
    • Retention period : 6 months
  • Records on contract or subscription withdrawal
    • Reasons for preservation: Act on Consumer Protection in Electronic Commerce Transactions, etc.
    • Retention period : 5 years
  • Records on payment and supply of goods, etc.
    • Reasons for preservation: Act on Consumer Protection in Electronic Commerce Transactions, etc.
    • Retention period : 5 years
  • Records on consumer complaints or dispute settlement
    • Reasons for preservation: Act on Consumer Protection in Electronic Commerce Transactions, etc.
    • Retention period : 3 years

4. Personal information destruction procedure and methoda

In principle, personal information of users is destroyed without delay when the purpose of collecting and using personal information is achieved. The procedure and method of destroying personal information are as follows:
  • Destruction Procedure
    • The information entered by the user for membership registration, etc., is transferred to a separate DB (separate filing cabinet in the case of paper) after the purpose is achieved, and is scheduled according to the reason for information protection according to internal policies and other related laws (refer to retention and use period) It is destroyed after the period is saved.
  • Method of destruction
    • Personal information printed on paper is destroyed by shredding or incineration.
    • Personal information stored in the form of electronic files is deleted using a technical method that cannot reproduce the record.
  • Destruction of personal information of dormant accounts
    • In accordance with Article 29 of the Act of Promotion of Information and Communication Network Utilization and Information Protection, and Article 16 of the Enforcement Decree of the same Act, personal information of dormant accounts that have not used the service for one year after membership registration may be destroyed or stored separately.
    • The Company notifies users of dormant accounts up to 30 days before the expiration date, and the notification details are as follows:
      • Notification content: The fact that personal information is destroyed or stored separately, the date and time of destruction, and personal information to be destroyed
      • Notification method: email, phone, fax, etc.
    • The exceptions below can be retained without destruction even after 1 year.
      • In case a separate period is set by other laws
      • If the period is set differently at the request of the user

5. Sharing and providing personal information

The company provides users' personal information in "1. The purpose of collecting and using personal information" is used only to the extent notified, and in principle, personal information is not disclosed to the outside without the user's consent. However, the following cases are exceptions :
  • If the user has agreed in advance Before personal information is provided, the personal information provider, the purpose of personal information provision, the items of personal information provided, and the retention period are notified separately, and if the user disagrees, the user's personal information shall not be provided to a third party.
  • In accordance with the provisions of the law, or if there is a request of an investigative agency for the purpose of investigation in accordance with the procedures and methods prescribed by the law

6. Consignment of processing personal information

For the safety of personal information protection in consignment contracts, compliance with laws and regulations related to personal information protection, prohibition of provision of personal information to a third party, and liability in case of accidents are clearly stipulated, and the contents of the contract are kept in writing and electronically. The company's personal information consignment processing agency and contents of consignment work are as follows.
[Service provider consignment company]
  • Consignee : Hilineisp Co., LTd Consigned work details : Cloud Service
  • Consignee : Allatpay Co., LTd Consigned work details : Electronic payment service
  • Consignee : Whois Co., LTd Consigned work details : Hosting
  • Consignee : Catenoid Co., LTd Consigned work details : Video Player
  • Consignee : JB Logis Consigned work details : Storing and shipping items
  • Consignee : CJ Logistics Consigned work details : Shipping items

7. Matters concerning the installation, operation and rejection of automatic personal information collection devices

The company uses "cookies" that store and retrieve user information from time to time in order to provide personalized and customized services. Cookies are very small text files sent by the server used to operate the website to the user's browser and are stored on the user's computer's hard disk. Cookies are used to provide customized information optimized to users by analyzing the company's services and usage patterns used by users.

a) Purpose of use of cookies

  • Provides a targeted marketing and personalized service and offers Inclass login service by analyzing the access frequency and visit time of members and non-members, identifying users' tastes and interests, tracking traces and identifying the degree of participation in various events and the number of visits.
  • Users have the option of installing cookies. Therefore, the user may allow all cookies by setting options in the web browser, check each time a cookie is saved, or refuse to save all cookies. However, if you refuse to store cookies, some services of companies that require login may be difficult to use.

b) Methods to specify whether to allow installation of cookies

Internet Explorer web browser
  • Select [Internet Options] from the [Tools] menu at the top of the web browser.
  • Click the [Personal Information] tab.
  • You can set cookies for each site through [Site(S)], [Advanced(V)].
Chrome web browser
  • Select the [Settings] menu on the right side of the web browser.
  • [Show advanced settings] at the bottom of the screen.
  • You can set cookies by selecting [Content Settings] in the [Personal Information] tab.
  • If you refuse to save cookies, it may be difficult to use some services that require login.

8. Technical/administrative protection measures for personal information

The company takes the following technical/administrative measures to ensure safety so that personal information is not lost, stolen, leaked, altered or damaged in processing users' personal information.
  • Personal information encryption The company encrypts personal information such as passwords and payment methods according to the standards required by laws and regulations, and protects users' personal information by taking separate security measures such as encrypting files and transmission data for important data.
  • Countermeasures against hacking, etc.
    • The company is doing its best to prevent the leakage or damage of members' personal information by hacking or computer viruses.
    • The system is installed in an area where access is controlled from outside, and an intrusion prevention device is used and an intrusion detection system is installed to monitor 24 hours a day.
    • The vaccine program is updated periodically to prevent personal information from being infringed by applying it as soon as the vaccine is released if a virus suddenly appears.
    • Through encrypted communication, etc., personal information can be safely transmitted over the network.

b) Administrative protection measures

  • Minimization of handling staff and training
    • The company minimizes the number of employees handling personal information to the person in charge, and assigns and manages a separate password for this, and emphasizes compliance with the personal information handling policy through occasional training for the person in charge.
  • Operation of a dedicated organization for personal information protection
    • The company's personal information-related processing staff is limited to the person in charge, and the company always emphasizes compliance with the company's personal information processing policy by providing training to the person in charge.

9. User's rights and exercise method

The rights of users and legal representatives are protected as follows :
  • Users and legal representatives can view or modify their registered personal information at any time, and request termination of subscription.
  • You can directly view, correct or withdraw after going through the identity verification process by clicking : 'My Page > Member Information Management > Member Information Modification' for Inclass users or personal information of children under 14 years of age, and 'My Page > Member Information Management > Membership Withdrawal' for membership withdrawal (withdrawal of consent).
  • If a user requests correction of errors in personal information, the personal information will not be used or provided until the correction is completed. In addition, if the wrong personal information has already been provided to a third party, we will notify the third party of the correction result without delay so that the correction can be made.
  • The Company handles personal information that has been canceled or deleted at the request of a user or legal representative as specified in the ‚ÄúPersonal Information Retention and Use Period‚Äù and does not allow it to be viewed or used for any other purpose.

10. Personal information manager and consultation/report

The company appoints a personal information protection officer who is responsible for collecting opinions and handling complaints about personal information. You can report all personal information protection-related complaints arising out of using the company's services to the contact information of the person in charge of personal information protection. The company will provide prompt and sufficient answers to users' reports.
  • Personal Information Protection Officer Name : Hwang Jieun Affiliation/Title: CEO Contact: (+82)2-578-7787 Email: inclass@greysteingroup.com

11. Matters concerning changes to the personal information processing policy

If there is any addition, deletion or modification of the contents of the current personal information processing policy, it will be notified through the "Notice" on the website at least 7 days before the revision.

12. Civil petition service for personal information

You can report all personal information protection-related complaints arising from using the company's services to the person in charge of personal information management or the department in charge. The company will provide prompt and sufficient answers to users' reports. If you need to report or consult about personal information infringement, please contact the following organizations:
  • Organization Name : Supreme Prosecutors' Office Cyber Crime Investigation Homepage : www.spo.go.kr Contact : 118
  • Organization Name : Privacy Infringement Report Center Homepage : privacy.kisa.or.kr Contact : (+82)2-3480-3571
  • Organization Name : National Police Agency Cyber Terror Response Center Homepage : www.ctrc.go.kr Contact : 118
For matters not stipulated in this personal information processing policy, our terms and conditions will be applied first within the scope of related laws. This privacy policy will take effect from March 9, 2018. Effective date of personal information handling policy : March 9, 2018.
